There is an orphaned volume and there\n\t\t\t// is nothing we can do about it.\n\t\t\tstrerr := fmt.Sprintf(\"Error cleaning provisioned volume for claim %s: %v. Please delete manually.\", claimToClaimKey(claim), deleteErr)\n\t\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(strerr)\n\t\t\tctrl.eventRecorder.Event(claim, v1.EventTypeWarning, events.ProvisioningCleanupFailed, strerr)\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Volume provisioned for claim\", \"PVC\", klog.KObj(claim), \"volumeName\", volume.Name)\n\t\tmsg := fmt.Sprintf(\"Successfully provisioned volume %s using %s\", volume.Name, plugin.GetPluginName())\n\t\tctrl.eventRecorder.Event(claim, v1.EventTypeNormal, events.ProvisioningSucceeded, msg)\n\t}\n\treturn pluginName, nil\n}\n\n// provisionClaimOperationExternal provisions a volume using external provisioner async-ly\n// This method will be running in a standalone go-routine scheduled in \"provisionClaim\"\nfunc (ctrl *PersistentVolumeController) provisionClaimOperationExternal(\n\tctx context.Context,\n\tclaim *v1.PersistentVolumeClaim,","numLines":150,"startLine":1675,"totalLines":2040}}}

The plugin coordinates mounting, unmounting, attaching, and detaching operations.\\n\\n4. **CSI Mounter** (pkg/volume/csi/csi_mounter.go): The `csiMountMgr` type implements volume mounting functionality, calling NodePublishVolume and NodeStageVolume CSI operations.\\n\\n5. **CSI Block Mapper** (pkg/volume/csi/csi_block.go): The `csiBlockMapper` type handles block device mapping for CSI volumes.\\n\\n6. **CSI Node Info Manager** (pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go): Manages CSI driver node information and topology labels.\\n\\n7. **PersistentVolume Controller** (pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go): The `PersistentVolumeController` bridges CSI operations to the core storage API. Key provisioning methods include:\\n   - `provisionClaim()`: Coordinates provisioning decisions\\n   - `provisionClaimOperation()`: Handles in-tree provisioning\\n   - `provisionClaimOperationExternal()`: Handles external provisioning (including CSI provisioners)\\n   \\n   The controller also handles PersistentVolume binding, deletion, and reclamation.\\n\\n8. **PersistentVolume Controller Base** (pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller_base.go): Contains CSI migration logic that translates in-tree storage plugins to CSI driver names via the `CSINameTranslator` interface and `CSIMigratedPluginManager`.\\n\\n9. **Attach/Detach Controller** (pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go): The `AttachDetachController` integrates CSI drivers for volume attachment state management at the cluster level, using CSI driver and CSINode informers.\\n\\n10. **Volume Expansion Controller** (pkg/controller/volume/expand/expand_controller.go): The `ExpandController` coordinates volume expansion, including CSI driver-based expansion via CSI migration translation.\\n\\nThese components work together to provide a complete CSI integration:\\n- The PersistentVolumeController determines provisioning strategy and coordinates with external CSI provisioners\\n- The CSI plugin registers drivers and handles volume lifecycle operations\\n- The CSI attacher manages device attachment through VolumeAttachment resources\\n- The node-level components (csiMountMgr, csiBlockMapper) communicate with drivers via the CSI gRPC client\\n- Migration support allows in-tree plugins to be transparently handled as CSI drivers\\n- CSI drivers are discovered and registered dynamically through the RegistrationHandler\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
